commit f1175b32f6afd0b03d9bb48d13add0dce93d87bf
Author: drunken-monkey <drunken-monkey@users.noreply.github.com>
Date:   Wed Jan 28 14:38:21 2015 +0100

    Add exception handling
    
    See [#2414347](https://www.drupal.org/node/2414347): when deleting items but Solr isn't running, it seems the Solr backend throws an exception from `deleteItems()` that is not a `SearchApiException` and, therefore, not permitted there. The exception should be caught and re-wrapped instead.
    
    However, upon fixing this I saw that the code currently is never catching any Solarium exceptions (except in `ping()`), so this change is just a start, this needs to happen everywhere we use Solarium methods that can throw exceptions.

    Apache Solr Multilingual now supports seperate settings for each environment and search page.
    Therefore these patches needs to be applied against the apachsesolr module itself:
    
    http://drupal.org/files/1918012_SolrQuery_aware_of_SearchPageID.patch
    http://drupal.org/files/1918030_add_custom_settings_to_search_pages.patch
    
    These patches are not required, but recommended:
    
    http://drupal.org/files/1915418_index_bundle_in_dedicated_env.patch
    http://drupal.org/files/1915614_config_actions_indexing_all_writable_envs_0.patch
    http://drupal.org/files/1917400_avoid_multiple_identical_values.patch
